<script type="text/javascript">
	//create public API
	window.audi = window.audi || {};
	window.audi.api = window.audi.api || {};
	window.audi.api.lastConfiguration = window.audi.api.lastConfiguration || function() {
		var _storage = window.localStorage;
		if (!!_storage && _storage.lastConfiguration) {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(_storage.lastConfiguration);
			} catch (err) {
				console.warn(err);
				return false;
			}
		} else {
			return false;
		}
	};
</script>

		if (Browser.isIE){
			if (Browser.version <= 8){
				var onclick = function() {
					if (!document.getElementById("nm-browsernotification-close-input").checked) {

			}

			}
		}
